<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:смертельный.html>смерте́льный</a> (3993)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смертельный.html>смерте́льный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">smertélʹnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>mortal, deadly, lethal, fatal</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> death; death-defying
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:смертельный.html>смерте́льный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:трюк.html>трюк</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:смертельный.html>смерте́льный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:номер.html>но́мер</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>smertélʹnyj</b> trjuk, <b>smertélʹnyj</b> nómer</i> ― <span class="e-translation">death trick, death-defying stunt</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:смертельный.html>смерте́льный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:бой.html>бой</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>smertélʹnyj</b> boj</i> ― <span class="e-translation">internecine battle</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:смертный.html>сме́ртный</a> (16885)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смерть.html>смерть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">smertʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смертный.html>сме́ртный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">smértnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>mortal</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> death
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:смертный.html>сме́ртный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:час.html>час</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>smértnyj</b> čas</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>death</b> hour</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:смертный.html>сме́ртный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:приговор.html>пригово́р</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>smértnyj</b> prigovór</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>death</b> sentence; <b>death</b> warrant</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:смертный.html>сме́ртная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:казнь.html>казнь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>smértnaja</b> kaznʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">capital punishment, <b>death</b> penalty</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смертный.html>сме́ртный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">smértnyj</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смертный.html>сме́ртного</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смертный.html>сме́ртные</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смертный.html>сме́ртных</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>mortal <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">person susceptible to death</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:простой.html>просты́е</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:смертный.html>сме́ртные</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">prostýje <b>smértnyje</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">mere mortals</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***смерть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:смерть.html>смерть</a> (318)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">съмьрть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sŭmĭrtĭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*sъmьrtь</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смерть.html>смерть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">smertʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смерть.html>сме́рти</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смерть.html>сме́рти</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смерть.html>смерте́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>death
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:смерть.html>смерть</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ná smertʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">deadly; utterly</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>(<i>used emphatically with <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a></i>) dying for
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ему́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:смерть.html>сме́рть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:хотеться.html>хо́чется</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:курить.html>кури́ть</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Jemú <b>smértʹ kak</b> xóčetsja kurítʹ.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">He's <b>dying for</b> a smoke.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:смерч.html>смерч</a> (10437)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">смьрьчь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">smĭrĭčĭ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cloud</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognates include <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">сморка́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">smorkátʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to blow one's nose</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:морока.html>морок</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">morok</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">darkness, cloud, fog</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мрак.html>мрак</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mrak</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">darkness</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

</p>

***смести.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сместить.html>смести́</a> (24626)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сместить.html>смести́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">smestí</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сметать.html>смета́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to brush off, to sweep off, to wipe off</li>
<li>to carry away <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">by wind, etc.</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to destroy, to dispel, to eliminate</li>
<li>to collect into one place <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">by raking or sweeping</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***сметана.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сметана.html>сметана</a> (8858)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <small>[Term?]</small>, cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Slovene_language" class="extiw" title="w:Slovene language">Slovene</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sl">smetana</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Slovak_language" class="extiw" title="w:Slovak language">Slovak</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sk">smotana</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bulgarian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Bulgarian language">Bulgarian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="bg"><a href = vnd.unilang:сметана.html>сметана</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="bg-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">smetana</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. According to <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Max_Vasmer" class="extiw" title="w:Max Vasmer">Vasmer</a>, the Slavic words are unrelated to German <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Schmand, Schmant</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">sour milk</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. However, other scholars (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Jacob_Grimm" class="extiw" title="w:Jacob Grimm">Jacob Grimm</a>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/cs:V%C3%A1clav_Machek_(jazykov%C4%9Bdec)" class="extiw" title="w:cs:Václav Machek (jazykovědec)">Václav Machek</a>) consider <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Schmand, Schmant</i> to be a loanword from Slavic.<sup id="cite_ref-DW_1-0" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-DW-1"> | 1 | </a></sup> See <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Schmand</i> for more.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сметана.html>смета́на</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">smetána</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сметана.html>смета́ны</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сметана.html>смета́ны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сметана.html>смета́н</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>sour cream</li></ol>

<p><b>сме<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>та́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:женский.html>же́нский</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 1-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 1a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">смет-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">smet-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

</p>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*sъmě̀ti</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сметь.html>сметь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">smetʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:посметь.html>посме́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to dare, to make bold, to be so bold as to</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:смех.html>смех</a> (1262)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<ul><li>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*směxъ</i>. Cognate with <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смеяться.html>смея́ться</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">smejátʹsja</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to laugh at</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.</li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смех.html>смех</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">smex</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смех.html>сме́ха</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смех.html>сме́хи</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смех.html>сме́хов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>laugh, laughter
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:чуть.html>чуть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> усса́лся <a href = vnd.unilang:со.html>со́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:смех.html>сме́ху</a></b>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja čutʹ ne ussálsja só <b>smexu</b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I nearly pissed myself laughing.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:смех.html>смех</a></b> (<span title="написание в дореформенной орфографии" style="border-bottom: 1px dotted; cursor: help">дореформ.</span> <span style="font-family: | Palatino Linotype | ">смѣхъ</span>)
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:мужской.html>мужско́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 2-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 3a−  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка) |  <a href = vnd.unilang:форма.html>фо́рмы</a> мн. ч. предположительны <a href = vnd.unilang:или.html>или</a> неупотребимы.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-сме-</b>; суффикс: <b>-х</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смехотворный.html>смехотво́рный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">smexotvórnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)смехотво́рнее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)смехотво́рней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>ridiculous, ludicrous</li>
<li>small, insignificant</li></ol>

<p><b>сме́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>шан<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ный</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:прилагательное.html>Прилага́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1*a(1).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b>с-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-меш-</b>; суффиксы: <b>-а-нн</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ый</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">с-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мешать.html>меша́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mešátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смешать.html>смеша́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">smešátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мешать.html>меша́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смешивать.html>сме́шивать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to mix, to mingle, to blend
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:смешать.html>смеша́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:грязь.html>гря́зью</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>smešátʹ</b> s grjázʹju</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to trample in the mud; to drag through the mud</span></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms imperfective"><span class="defdate">Imperfectives:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мешать.html>меша́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">mešátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смешивать.html>сме́шивать</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">sméšivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>to mix up the order of
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:смешать.html>смеша́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:карта.html>ка́рты</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>smešátʹ</b> kárty</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to spoil/ruin someone's game; upset someone's plans</span></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms imperfective"><span class="defdate">Imperfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смешивать.html>сме́шивать</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">sméšivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">only</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to mess up
<dl><dd><span class="nyms imperfective"><span class="defdate">Imperfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смешивать.html>сме́шивать</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">sméšivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">only</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>to confuse, to mix up
<dl><dd><span class="nyms imperfective"><span class="defdate">Imperfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смешивать.html>сме́шивать</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">sméšivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">only</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

***смешаться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:смешаться.html>смеша́ться</a> (7451)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смешать.html>смеша́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">smešátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смешаться.html>смеша́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">smešátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мешаться.html>меша́ться</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смешиваться.html>сме́шиваться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to mix, to blend (in), to mingle, to intermingle with <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + instrumental</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:смешаться.html>смеша́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:толпа.html>толпо́й</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>smešátʹsja</b> s tolpój</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to mingle/merge with the crowd</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to merge</li>
<li>to get mixed up, to be jumbled</li>
<li>to become confused</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смешать.html>смеша́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">smešátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смешить.html>смеши́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">smešítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<ol><li>in a funny manner/way, comically</li>

</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смешной.html>смешно́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">smešnój</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)смешне́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)смешне́й</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>funny, comic, droll</li>
<li>laughable, ridiculous, ludicrous</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:смещение.html>смеще́ние</a> (13763)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сместить.html>смести́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">smestítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смещение.html>смеще́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">smeščénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смещение.html>смеще́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смещение.html>смеще́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смещение.html>смеще́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>displacement, shift</li></ol>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b>сме<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ще́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ни.html>ни</a><span class="hyph-dot" style="color:red;">·</span>е</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:средний.html>сре́дний</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 2-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 7a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b>с-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-мещ-</b>; суффикс: <b>-ениj</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-е</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
